<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">PART&nbsp;I</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1.<i>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Business</i></font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Overview</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We are a medical device company specializing in innovative technologies for the cardiac and vascular markets.&#160; Our key strategic growth initiative is our newest marketable product, RenalGuard</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">RenalGuard is designed to reduce the potentially toxic effects that contrast media can have on the kidneys when it is administered to patients during certain medical imaging procedures. It is believed that allowing contrast media to dwell in the kidneys of certain higher risk patients can lead to contrast-induced nephropathy (&#147;CIN&#148;), a potentially deadly form of acute kidney injury. By inducing and maintaining a high urine flow rate before, during and after these medical imaging procedures, we believe the incidence rates of CIN in at-risk patients can be reduced. RenalGuard facilitates this increased urine clearance automatically, enabling the body to more rapidly void the contrast media, thereby reducing its overall resident time and toxic effects in the kidney.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The RenalGuard System consists of a proprietary console and accompanying single-use sets. RenalGuard operates by first collecting and measuring patient urine outputs and then in real-time precisely matching these urine outputs with a prescribed replacement fluid by means of intravenous infusion. With its automated matched fluid replacement capability, RenalGuard is intended to promote and maintain high urine outputs and minimize the risk to patients of over- or under-hydration during image-guided catheterization procedures where contrast media are routinely administered.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We obtained a CE Mark for RenalGuard in December&nbsp;2007 and began our initial commercialization efforts in the European Union (&#147;EU&#148;) in Italy in April&nbsp;2008. Since then, we have expanded our sales efforts for RenalGuard to other countries in the EU and additional countries around the world where we have received the necessary approvals to do so. In the U.S. we must first successfully complete a pivotal clinical study assessing the safety and effectiveness of RenalGuard in reducing the rates of CIN in at-risk patients and obtain U.S. Food and Drug Administration (&#147;FDA&#148;) pre-market approval in order to market RenalGuard. We expect to commence this pivotal clinical trial of RenalGuard in 2011.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Recent Developments</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Sale of TMR Business to Novadaq</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Prior to February&nbsp;1, 2011, including during all of 2010 and 2009, in addition to advancing our RenalGuard program, we also were engaged in the manufacture and marketing of the <i>CO</i></font><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:1.0pt;">2</font></i><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&#160;Heart Laser System</font></i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> that cardiac surgeons use to perform carbon dioxide (CO</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:1.0pt;">2</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">) transmyocardial revascularization, or TMR, to alleviate symptoms of severe angina. On February&nbsp;1, 2011, we completed an asset sale transaction and sold our TMR business to Novadaq Corp. (&#147;Novadaq&#148;), a subsidiary of Novadaq Technologies Inc. [TSX: NDQ]. Novadaq acted as our exclusive distributor in the United States for our TMR business since being appointed to that role in March&nbsp;2007.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The asset sale transaction, which was announced in November&nbsp;2010, was approved by our shareholders at a special meeting on January&nbsp;31, 2011 and the transaction closed on February&nbsp;1, 2011. Novadaq paid $1 million in cash and assumed all our TMR service-related obligations, valued at approximately $614,000, in exchange for acquiring substantially all our TMR-related assets, including all regulatory approvals for the <i>CO</i></font><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:1.0pt;">2</font></i><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&#160;Heart Laser System</font></i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">, all manufacturing rights, substantially all product inventories and all equipment, intellectual property, clinical data and documentation related to our TMR business. The sale of the TMR business and the resultant gain on the asset sale transaction will be recorded in our first quarter 2011 financial results.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Secured Convertible Debt Financing</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On February&nbsp;22, 2011, we completed a financing agreement with an institutional investor that provides us with up to $6 million in secured convertible debt financing. We received $4 million in February&nbsp;as part of a first tranche closing. In addition, under the terms of the financing agreement, we may secure additional secured convertible debt</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1<a name="PB_1_053655_5796"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">funding of up to $2 million in the aggregate in two separate $1 million tranches, based upon meeting certain RenalGuard operational milestones related to sales and U.S. pivotal clinical trial objectives.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the terms of this financing, we issued senior secured convertible notes that mature three years from date of issuance as well as warrants exercisable for a period of five years from the date of issuance for an aggregate number of shares equal to the aggregate number of shares issuable upon conversion of the notes. The notes issued in the February&nbsp;2011 first tranche funding are convertible at a rate of $.10 per share. The notes that would be issued in the future for each of the $1 million tranches would be convertible into our common stock at prices determined by the fair market value of our stock at the time each tranche funds, subject to an agreed-upon minimum and maximum conversion rate price range of $.06&#160; to $.15.&#160; The notes carry a 5% interest coupon that is required to be paid quarterly and are secured by all of our assets. The warrants can be converted into our common stock as well, at a 50% premium to the conversion price of the notes, which would also vary depending upon the tranche. The conversion price of the notes and the exercise price of the warrants are subject to anti-dilution and other adjustments.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">RenalGuard Program</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our near term focus for our RenalGuard program is to (1)&nbsp;establish a broader distribution network in the EU and countries outside the EU where we have the approval to market RenalGuard, (2)&nbsp;assist our distributors in their ongoing efforts to sell RenalGuard and increase adoption and use of our technology, (3)&nbsp;continue support of two investigator-sponsored studies utilizing RenalGuard that have been conducted in Italy, as well as any others that may arise, and leverage the positive data from those studies to drive additional RenalGuard sales, as well as help us to raise additional capital in the future and (4)&nbsp;commence our U.S. pivotal clinical trial of RenalGuard.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Italian Clinical Studies</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The first of two investigator-sponsored studies in Italy, the MYTHOS trial, is a randomized, open-label controlled clinical trial conducted at the Centro Cardiologico Monzino-University of Milan (&#147;CCM&#148;) in Milan,&nbsp;Italy. The MYTHOS trial is designed to determine the safety and effectiveness of RenalGuard in preventing CIN in at-risk patients. The study was originally designed to enroll 120 patients, which was achieved in January&nbsp;2010. The study was expanded to enroll additional patients in order to obtain stronger and more meaningful statistical data on the safety and effectiveness of RenalGuard in reducing the incidence rate of CIN.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The most recent data that has been released on the results of the MYTHOS trial is based upon the first 157 patients enrolled in the study. These interim results strongly support both RenalGuard&#146;s safety profile and its high degree of efficacy in reducing the rates of CIN in at-risk patients. In the RenalGuard-treated group, the incidence rate of CIN was only 5%, 69% lower than the 16% CIN rate recorded in the control group. The RenalGuard-treated group also experienced a statistically significant fewer number of in-hospital major adverse events.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The MYTHOS investigators are preparing a manuscript summarizing the clinical trial results, which they plan to submit for publication.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The second investigator-sponsored study, the REMEDIAL II trial, is a multi-center, randomized, open-label controlled clinical trial based at the Clinica Mediterranea in Naples,&nbsp;Italy and three other hospitals in Italy. The interim results reported on the first 123 patients also demonstrate strong efficacy, with a 3.2% CIN rate in the RenalGuard treated group, 75% lower than the 13% CIN rate in the control group. The investigators have informed us they have completed patient enrollment and their abstract summarizing the latest study results has been accepted for presentation at the upcoming 60</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">th</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;Annual Scientific Session of the American College of Cardiology in April&nbsp;2011.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We hope that the continued release and publication of positive scientific data from the MYTHOS and REMEDIAL II clinical trials will both increase the adoption rate of our RenalGuard technology and enable us to continue to raise the additional capital we will need to advance our RenalGuard program in the future.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">U.S.</font></i></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">  <i>Clinical Trial</i></font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">RenalGuard is currently an investigational device in the U.S.&#160; In December&nbsp;2006, we received FDA approval to conduct our first human clinical trial utilizing RenalGuard under an investigational device exemption (&#147;IDE&#148;). This pilot</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2<a name="PB_2_053726_2897"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">
<hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left">
</font></b></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\tfort\11-2116-1\task4579433\2116-1-bc.htm',USER='tfort',CD='Mar 29 08:44 2011' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">clinical trial was designed to evaluate the safety of RenalGuard and the ability of our RenalGuard System to accurately measure and balance fluid inputs and outputs on up to 40 patients undergoing a catheterization imaging procedure where contrast media would be administered.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We enrolled a total of 23 patients in this pilot study. Based upon the positive safety data collected in the study and discussions with the FDA, we elected to stop enrolling new patients in the pilot study in November&nbsp;2007.&#160; We submitted an IDE supplement to the FDA in February&nbsp;2008 seeking approval to move from our pilot study to a pivotal clinical trial to study the safety and effectiveness of RenalGuard in the prevention of CIN. In November&nbsp;2008, the FDA granted us approval to begin our pivotal study, but we deferred commencing this study until we could raise the necessary additional capital needed to conduct the study. We expect to commence this pivotal U.S. clinical trial of RenalGuard in 2011 with the funds obtained from the recent sale of our TMR business and the $4 million institutional financing we secured in February&nbsp;2011.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have submitted an updated clinical trial protocol to the FDA for the U.S. clinical study of RenalGuard and must obtain FDA approval for this planned study prior to enrolling the first patient in the study.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">CIN</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The diagnosis and treatment of cardiovascular disease rely heavily on cardiovascular imaging.&#160; Interventional cardiologists and radiologists are increasingly becoming involved at earlier stages in the management and treatment of patients suffering from cardiovascular disease, as noninvasive imaging and interventional treatment techniques, such as angioplasty procedures and stent placements, increase in demand and outpace the use of invasive surgical options.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We estimate that approximately seven million cardiovascular diagnostic and interventional imaging procedures are performed worldwide each year.&#160; These less invasive, image-guided medical procedures require the use of an iodine-based radiocontrast media, or dye, to facilitate the capture and display of x-ray images. These contrast agents are known to be toxic to the kidneys, whose main function is to filter and remove wastes and fluids, such as this dye, from the body. Patients who undergo a diagnostic or interventional imaging procedure and who present themselves with a certain level of pre-existing impaired renal (kidney) function are especially susceptible to the toxic effects of these contrast agents and to developing CIN.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We believe CIN is a major and growing problem due to the increasing number of older patients, diabetics and patients with pre-existing renal impairment requiring interventional procedures that use radiographic contrast media. CIN is the third most common cause of in-hospital acute renal failure. It is associated with increased in-hospital mortality rates, and increases in long-term mortality, major in-hospital adverse cardiac events, and risk of renal dialysis therapy.&#160; Any of these can result in prolonged hospital stays and increased medical costs.&#160; We believe that approximately 10% to 20% of all patients undergoing image-guided cardiology and radiology procedures are at risk of developing CIN. The estimated mortality rate for patients who develop CIN may be as high as 35%.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Potential Market Size</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based upon a market research study that was performed for us as well as other sources, we estimate that there are approximately 4 million diagnostic and interventional cardiology and radiology imaging procedures requiring the use of contrast agents that are performed annually in the U.S. alone, and an estimated 7 million worldwide.&#160; Patients with other significant risk factors besides renal insufficiency, such as congestive heart failure, anemia, peripheral vascular disease, diabetes and being over the age of 75, are also at risk for developing CIN.&#160; This population continues to grow. Specifically, the Heart Disease and Stroke Statistics &#151; 2011 Update, or 2011 HSSU, which was published by the American Heart Association, estimates that there were 171 million individuals with diabetes worldwide in 2000 and that number is projected to rise to 366 million by 2030.&#160; It is estimated that nearly 26 million people in the U.S. have chronic kidney disease (&#147;CKD&#148;) and another 20 million are at increased risk for CKD.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At-risk patients with renal insufficiency are easily identified with a routine blood analysis involving the level of a waste product in the blood called serum creatinine and an industry-standard calculation called a creatinine clearance.&#160; Creatinine clearance can be accurately calculated using serum creatinine concentration and some or all of the following variables: sex, age, weight and race, as suggested by the National Kidney Foundation.&#160; A decrease in creatinine clearance is generally accepted as a good indicator of kidney disease.&#160; CIN is usually defined as an increase in serum creatinine of</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3<a name="PB_3_053819_3020"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">
<hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left">
</font></b></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\JMS\tfort\11-2116-1\task4579433\2116-1-bc.htm',USER='tfort',CD='Mar 29 08:44 2011' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">25% over baseline within four days of a procedure where contrast is administered.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Of the estimated 7 million diagnostic and interventional imaging procedures performed worldwide each year that involve the use of contrast agents, we believe that 15% of these cases, or approximately 1 million patients, could be considered at-risk for CIN and thus benefit from the use of RenalGuard.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">RenalGuard Sales and Marketing</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We obtained a CE Mark for RenalGuard in December&nbsp;2007 and began our initial commercialization efforts in the EU in Italy in April&nbsp;2008. Since then, we have expanded our sales efforts for RenalGuard to other countries in the EU and additional countries around the world where we have received the necessary approvals to do so.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To date we have relied exclusively on independent distributors to sell our product into international markets and we expect to continue this sales strategy for the foreseeable future. Distributors who we contract with to market our product typically also represent at least several other company product lines and have demonstrated experience selling their full spectrum of products into cardiovascular centers throughout their territory. Our distribution agreements typically set forth minimum annual purchase requirements over the term of the contract, although these annual minimums may be waived by us in our sole discretion. Typically our distribution agreements provide our distributors the exclusive right to market our products in a specific territory and generally have a duration that ranges between three and five years.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our international distributors determine the programs, including sale, lease, rental and usage-based offerings, which they believe will be most effective in selling our products to hospitals in their territory. Our distributors&#146; marketing efforts are directed primarily at interventional cardiologists and nephrologists, whose influence are both believed to be critical in a hospital&#146;s decision to acquire our products.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the U.S., we must first successfully complete a pivotal clinical study assessing the safety and effectiveness of RenalGuard in reducing the rates of CIN in at-risk patients and obtain FDA pre-market approval in order to market RenalGuard.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">RenalGuard System and Therapy</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">RenalGuard is designed to reduce the toxic effects that contrast media can have on the kidneys, which may lead to a reduction in the incidence of CIN in at-risk patients.&#160; RenalGuard Therapy</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;is based upon existing published literature, including the industry-recognized PRINCE study, that supports the theory that inducing and maintaining high urine output through the kidneys allows the body to rapidly eliminate contrast, reducing its toxic effects.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our RenalGuard System is a real-time automated measurement and matched fluid replacement device.&#160; The system is comprised of a fluid balancing system and a console with a delivery mechanism for sterile replacement fluid, including detectors, monitors and alarms. It is a closed loop system where the urine produced by the patient through a standard Foley-type catheter is continuously measured. A unique sterile disposable kit is required for each procedure.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our RenalGuard Therapy entails the use of a standard FDA-approved loop diuretic that induces the required high urine output that is measured and in real-time replaced with an equal volume of sterile solution, such as saline, by the RenalGuard System.&#160; This matched fluid replacement is intended to minimize the risk of over- or under-hydration, which can lead to increased patient risks, including pulmonary edema </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> a swelling and/or fluid accumulation in the lungs that leads to impaired gas exchange and may cause respiratory failure.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Potential Benefits of RenalGuard</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We are attempting to bring RenalGuard to market as the first product to address this problem.&#160; We believe it is a safe, innovative technology capable of achieving significant market adoption due to its evidence-based therapy and straightforward integration into hospital environments where contrast agents are routinely used.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_053854_7748"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">
<hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left">
</font></b></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\tfort\11-2116-1\task4579433\2116-1-bc.htm',USER='tfort',CD='Mar 29 08:44 2011' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Evidence-based Therapy</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our RenalGuard Therapy has now been studied in two randomized, open-label controlled clinical trials. The aim of these studies is to determine if very high urine outputs with precise matching of intravascular volume significantly reduced the risk of CIN.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The positive results to date reported from these studies have given us confidence that our concept of inducing high urine output with matched fluid replacement to maintain intravascular volume can significantly reduce the incidence of CIN.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Straightforward Hospital Integration</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We believe RenalGuard can easily be integrated into hospital environments where contrast agents are routinely used.&#160; It leverages existing hospital resources to protect at-risk patients within the current therapy window. RenalGuard is designed to be simple to operate and to have features that are similar to devices currently used by hospital staff, and because it is automated, it lessens the burden on staff to constantly monitor patients.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Other Potential Markets</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We plan to focus our short-term marketing efforts on the interventional cardiovascular and radiology markets and the reduction of CIN in imaging procedures requiring the use of contrast. In addition, we believe that our RenalGuard Therapy and System may be attractive to hospitals as an automated fluid balancing system that could be used in certain intensive patient monitoring settings within the hospital, such as the intensive care unit, or where fluid management is critical, such as in post-kidney transplant patients where the replacement of fluid losses is necessary to avoid the risk of damage to the transplanted kidney.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Current Treatment Methods for CIN</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The only clinically accepted and routinely utilized preventive measure for patients at risk for CIN is pre- and post- procedure overnight hydration, which is inconvenient, expensive and time-consuming for hospital staff. There is currently no FDA-approved device or drug for CIN prevention. Due to the attractiveness of the potential market, we believe that there are a number of other companies developing or investigating potential new CIN preventive drugs, devices and therapies.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Preventive measures being used in clinical practice today include:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Mucomyst</font></i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">N-acetylcysteine (Mucomyst</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">) is both a renal vasodilator and antioxidant.&#160; It is prescribed by a doctor prior to the start of an interventional procedure and is taken by the patient in prearranged doses that may start the day before the procedure.&#160; This therapy is employed by most physicians due to an extremely low risk profile and cost.&#160; Clinical data linking Mucomyst to a reduction in CIN is to date inconclusive.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Sodium bicarbonate</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sodium bicarbonate is a pre-mixed pharmaceutical solution that is given intravenously on the same day as the procedure, prior to the start.&#160; Currently, there are only a small number of published studies that have evaluated utilizing sodium bicarbonate as a preventive measure.&#160; There is some industry adoption of this measure to reduce the incidence of CIN simply due to the lack of expense and low risk to patients.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Device-Based Competition</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In January&nbsp;2009, AngioDynamics Inc. acquired certain assets of FlowMedica,&nbsp;Inc., including its Benephit</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;CV Infusion System, which is a catheter designed to deliver drugs and/or fluid directly to the renal arteries during an interventional procedure.&#160; This system is FDA 510(k)-cleared and CE-marked for the infusion of physician-specified agents in the peripheral vasculature.&#160; We believe market challenges for this approach may include concerns regarding</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_053930_141"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">
<hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left">
</font></b></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\JMS\tfort\11-2116-1\task4579433\2116-1-bc.htm',USER='tfort',CD='Mar 29 08:44 2011' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">complications of direct renal intervention and the cost of the catheter.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">The CO</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:bold;position:relative;top:1.0pt;">2</font></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;Heart Laser System</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">TMR is performed by a cardiovascular surgeon, who uses a laser to create channels through the myocardium of the heart in an attempt to restore perfusion to areas of the heart not being reached by diseased or clogged arteries. This technique is used for relief of symptoms of severe angina in patients with ischemic heart disease not amenable to direct coronary revascularization interventions, such as angioplasty, stenting or coronary artery bypass grafting (bypass surgery). In addition to providing new direct pathways for blood to reach the ischemic myocardium, the creation of TMR channels is also believed to promote angiogenesis, the development of new blood vessels.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In August&nbsp;1998, we received approval from the FDA to market our first generation CO</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:1.0pt;">2</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;Heart Laser, the HL1, throughout the U.S.&#160; In January&nbsp;2001, we received approval from the FDA to market our smaller and lighter second generation CO</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:1.0pt;">2</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;Heart Laser, the HL2.&#160; The FDA approved the use of the Heart Laser Systems for patients who have stable angina (Canadian Cardiovascular Society Class&nbsp;III or IV) refractory to medical treatment and secondary to objectively demonstrated coronary artery atherosclerosis and with a region of the myocardium not amenable to direct coronary revascularization.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each TMR procedure requires a sterile, single-use TMR kit containing assorted TMR handpieces, drapes and other disposable items. The HL1 and HL2 lasers each require this TMR kit as part of the system.&#160; The same TMR kit may be used with either the HL1 or HL2 laser.&#160; The combination of either an HL1 or an HL2 with a TMR kit is referred to throughout this annual report on Form&nbsp;10-K as the Heart Laser System.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As previously discussed, on February&nbsp;1, 2011, we sold substantially all of our TMR-related assets to Novadaq, including all regulatory approvals for the Heart Laser System, all manufacturing rights, substantially all product inventories and all equipment, intellectual property, clinical data and documentation related to our TMR business.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">TMR Sales and Marketing Strategy</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On March&nbsp;20, 2007, we appointed Novadaq to succeed Edwards Lifesciences LLC (&#147;Edwards&#148;) as our exclusive U.S. distributor for the HL2 and all TMR disposable procedure kits. Outside the U.S., we established an independent distributor network to market our TMR products, although in some areas, principally Europe, we continued to sell our TMR products directly to hospitals.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">International sales (by origin) accounted for 13% of our total revenue in 2010 and 29% in 2009.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We sold our TMR products to both Novadaq and our international distributors at a discount off list price.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Marketing Programs</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As the exclusive U.S. distributor of our TMR products, Novadaq determined the programs, including sale, lease, rental and usage-based offerings, that it believed would be most effective in the U.S. in selling our products to hospitals. Novadaq&#146;s marketing efforts were directed primarily at cardiothoracic surgeons, whose influence is believed to be critical in a hospital&#146;s decision to purchase our products.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">TMR Competition</font></i></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The only direct competitor in the TMR market at this time is CardioGenesis Corporation.&#160; CardioGenesis has received FDA approval to market its holmium laser in the U.S. to perform TMR.&#160; CardioGenesis has also received CE Mark approval for its TMR system, which allows it to sell its product commercially in the EU.&#160; CardioGenesis promotes the advantages it believes its TMR system provides surgeons who wish to perform minimally-invasive or robotically-assisted TMR procedures.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Products and Customers</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales and servicing of our Heart Laser Systems accounted for approximately 85% and 76% of our revenues for</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6<a name="PB_6_054007_7608"></a></font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">
<hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left">
</font></b></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='6',FILE='C:\JMS\tfort\11-2116-1\task4579433\2116-1-bc.htm',USER='tfort',CD='Mar 29 08:44 2011' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2010 and 2009, respectively. RenalGuard sales accounted for approximately 9% and 12% of our revenues for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2010 and 2009, respectively.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our U.S. TMR distributor, Novadaq, was our largest customer the past two years and accounted for 76% and 65% of our total revenues in the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2010 and 2009, respectively. Our distributor of RenalGuard in Italy, Artech, accounted for 4% and 10% of our total revenues in the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2010 and 2009, respectively and 48% and 81% of our RenalGuard revenues in the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2010 and 2009, respectively.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Manufacturing</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During 2010 and 2009 we manufactured and tested our Heart Laser System and our RenalGuard console at our facility in Franklin, Massachusetts.&#160; Beginning in 2011 we expect both our RenalGuard consoles and sterile disposable kits will be manufactured for us by two separate outside contract manufacturers, both located in New England. We believe that our outside contract manufacturers will have sufficient capacity to meet market demands anticipated in the coming year for our RenalGuard product.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our facilities and those of our outside contract manufacturers are subject to periodic inspection by regulatory authorities to ensure compliance with FDA and EU quality system regulations.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Government Regulation</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">RenalGuard and the Heart Laser Systems both are subject to extensive regulation by the FDA and other regulatory authorities in the U.S. and abroad.&#160; The Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act (the &#147;FDC Act&#148;) and other federal and state statutes and regulations govern the research, design, development, manufacturing, preclinical and clinical testing, installation, storage, packaging, recordkeeping, servicing, labeling, distribution and promotion of medical devices in the U.S.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a device manufacturer, we are also required to register with the FDA.&#160; As such, we are subject to inspection on a routine basis for compliance with the FDA&#146;s Quality Systems regulations.&#160; These regulations require that we manufacture our products and maintain our documents in a prescribed manner with respect to manufacturing, testing and control activities.&#160; Further, we are required to comply with various FDA requirements for reporting.&#160; The FDC Act and medical device reporting regulations require that we provide information to the FDA on deaths or serious injuries alleged to have been caused or contributed to by the use of our products, as well as product malfunctions that would likely cause or contribute to death or serious injury if the malfunction were to recur.&#160; The FDA also prohibits an approved device from being marketed for unapproved uses.&#160; Our product promotion and advertising is subject to continuing FDA regulation.&#160; Our laser products are subject to periodic inspection under the radiation health and safety provisions of the FDC Act for compliance with labeling and other safety regulations.&#160; The failure to comply with the applicable regulatory requirements may subject us to a variety of administrative or judicially imposed sanctions, including the FDA&#146;s refusal to approve pending or supplemental applications, withdrawal of an approval or clearance, warning letters, product recalls, product seizures, total or partial suspension of production or distribution, injunctions, fines, and civil and criminal penalties against that company or its officers, directors or employees.&#160; Failure to comply with regulatory requirements could have a material adverse effect on our business, financial condition and results of operations.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">From time to time, legislation is drafted and introduced in Congress that could significantly change the statutory provisions governing the approval, manufacturing and marketing of drug products and medical devices.&#160; In addition, FDA regulations and guidance are often revised or reinterpreted by the agency in ways that may significantly affect our business and our products.&#160; It is impossible to predict whether legislative changes will be enacted, or FDA regulations, guidance, or interpretations changed, and what the impact of such changes, if any, may be.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Various foreign countries in which our products are or may be sold impose additional or different regulatory and testing requirements. The international regulatory approval process varies from country to country and is subject to change in a given country as regulatory requirements change.&#160; Thus, the time required for an approval may differ and there can be substantial delays in obtaining approval after the relevant applications are filed.&#160; There is no assurance that foreign regulatory authorities will approve the use or sale of our products in a particular country on a timely basis, or at all.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Proprietary Processes, Patents, Licenses and Other Rights</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It is our practice to file patent applications to protect our technology, inventions and product improvements. We also rely on trade secret protection for certain confidential and proprietary information.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have been issued 5 U.S. patents and 1 Canadian patent related to our RenalGuard System and its use in preventing CIN.&#160; These patents have terms that expire from 2026 through 2028.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition, we currently have eight patent applications pending at the U.S. Patent Office in connection with the prevention of CIN related to RenalGuard. We have international patent applications pending on six of these RenalGuard patents, including individual patent applications pending in the EU and Japan.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Although we believe our patents to be strong, litigation by a competitor seeking to invalidate these patents could have a material adverse effect on our business, financial condition and results of operations.&#160; No assurance can be given that the existing patents will be held valid if challenged, that any additional patents will be issued or that the scope of any patent protection will exclude competitors.&#160; The breadth of claims in medical technology patents involves complex legal and factual issues and therefore can be highly uncertain.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We also rely upon unpatented proprietary technology and trade secrets that we seek to protect, in part, through confidentiality agreements with employees and other parties.&#160; No assurance can be given that these agreements will not be breached, that we will have adequate remedies for any breach, that others will not independently develop or otherwise acquire substantially equivalent proprietary technology and trade secrets or disclose such technology or that we can meaningfully protect our rights in such unpatented technology.&#160; In addition, others may hold or receive patents that contain claims covering products developed by us.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We believe our patents to be valid and enforceable.&#160; However, there has been substantial litigation regarding patent and other intellectual property rights in the medical device industry.&#160; Litigation, which could result in substantial cost and diversion of our efforts, may be necessary to enforce our patents, to protect our trade secrets, to defend ourselves against claimed infringement of the rights of others and to determine the scope and validity of the proprietary rights of others.&#160; Adverse determinations in litigation could subject us to significant liabilities to third parties, require us to seek licenses from third parties and prevent us from manufacturing, selling or using our products, any of which could have a material adverse effect on our business, financial condition and results of operations.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Research and Development</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Research and development expenses were approximately $333,000 and $780,000 for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2010 and 2009, respectively.&#160; Our current and near term development efforts will be focused exclusively on advancing our RenalGuard program.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We continue to monitor technologies that may be applicable to the market for CIN</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> prevention</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.&#160; No assurance can be given that our research and development goals will be implemented successfully.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Employees</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of March&nbsp;17, 2011, we had 8 full-time employees worldwide, including our executive officers. Of these, four are in general and administrative positions, two are involved in sales and customer support, one is involved in clinical/research and development and one is involved in manufacturing/regulatory affairs.&#160; None of our employees are represented by a union.&#160; We consider our relationship with our employees to be good.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Company Information</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We were incorporated in British Columbia, Canada on March&nbsp;3, 1987.&#160; We transferred our jurisdiction of incorporation to the Yukon Territory of Canada in March&nbsp;1999.&#160; Our principal offices and manufacturing facilities are located at 10 Forge Park, Franklin, Massachusetts 02038.&#160; Our telephone number is (508) 541-8800.&#160; Our Internet address is <i>www.plcmed.com</i>.&#160; As used herein, the references to PLC, we, our and the Company mean, unless the context </font></p>

The total base rental payments for the eight months ending August&nbsp;31, 2011 is approximately $136,000.&#160; We are also responsible for certain operating and maintenance costs and real estate taxes.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Dividends</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have never paid cash dividends.&#160; We currently intend to retain all future earnings, if any, for use in our business and we do not anticipate paying any cash dividends in the foreseeable future. The terms of our secured convertible debt financing prohibits the payment of any cash dividends without the prior written consent of the holders of a majority of the principal amount of the outstanding convertible notes.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Securities Authorized for Issuance Under Equity Compensation Plans</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following table provides information about the securities authorized for issuance under our equity compensation plans as of December&nbsp;31, 2010:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="93%" style="border-collapse:collapse;margin-left:.25in;width:93.34%;">
<tr>
<td width="29%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:29.28%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Plan&nbsp;Category</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.14%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="20%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:20.36%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(a)<br>   Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;securities&nbsp;to<br>   be&nbsp;issued&nbsp;upon&nbsp;exercise<br>   of&nbsp;outstanding&nbsp;options,<br>   warrants&nbsp;and&nbsp;rights</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.14%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="20%" colspan="2" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:20.36%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(b)<br>   Weighted-average<br>   exercise&nbsp;price&nbsp;of<br>   outstanding&nbsp;options,<br>   warrants&nbsp;and&nbsp;rights</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.14%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 21.75pt;text-indent:-21.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Consists of the following equity compensation plans: (i)&nbsp;2000 Employee Stock Purchase Plan, as amended (the &#147;2000 ESPP&#148;); (ii) 2000 Equity Incentive Plan; and (iii)&nbsp;2005 Stock Incentive Plan.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 21.75pt;text-indent:-21.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
